	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'ed07201726d46662db877cd55291d283867d8126') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'ed07201726d46662db877cd55291d283867d8126') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'f47e42d0f5c0fdef466f6207e5906e7024f69174') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'ed07201726d46662db877cd55291d283867d8126') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');

	}

	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != 'b6dee270c8edb1738832c4ae1579c33e607ff0e0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'b6dee270c8edb1738832c4ae1579c33e607ff0e0') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'a2850767f986f0992708a76997fbde2f552a9f0b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'b6dee270c8edb1738832c4ae1579c33e607ff0e0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '5a7388f028ef5eb1faa5b28f09e6606f96aded55') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5a7388f028ef5eb1faa5b28f09e6606f96aded55') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c958f97fabb5dd7f890a3590b3e7ed18ba1bf0fc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5a7388f028ef5eb1faa5b28f09e6606f96aded55') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') != '04f971dfc2a2d0251dbf5f97426c33c4c02ad018') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== '04f971dfc2a2d0251dbf5f97426c33c4c02ad018') {

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

				warn('Creation of backup failed');
